Kaiser Basics

Active Realign: Defender Mode
Master Level 1
Description Switches from offensive to defensive mode. Passive enhancements increase at higher Job Advancements. Skill enhancements stack.
Level 1 Defense: +200


Active Realign: Attacker Mode
Master Level 1
Description Switches from defensive to offensive mode. Passive enhancements increase at higher Job Advancements. Skill enhancements stack.
Level 1 Attack Power: +5, Critical Rate: +3%, Boss Damage: +3%


Active Vertical Grapple
Master Level 1
Description Fires a grappling hook to a platform above you to ascend quickly.
Level 1 Press the skill key while you're climbing to cancel.


Passive Transfiguration
Master Level 1
Description Increases Speed, Jump, and Knockback Resistance with Dragon Warrior strength.
Level 1 Movement Speed +10, Jump +20, Knockback Resistance +40%
Show/hide all levels
Passive Iron Will
Master Level 3
Description Kaiser's iron will grants additional HP and increases damage depending on the Morph Gauge Stage. Only the HP increase is applied when used as a Link Skill.
Level 1 Max HP: +5%, Damage increase per Morph Gauge Stage: +2%
3 Max HP: +15%, Damage increase per Morph Gauge Stage: +4%
Passive Iron Will
Master Level 3
Description Kaiser's iron will grants additional HP and increases damage depending on the Morph Gauge Stage. Only the HP increase is applied when used as a Link Skill.
Level 1 Max HP: +5%, Damage increase per Morph Gauge Stage: +2%
2 Max HP: +10%, Damage increase per Morph Gauge Stage: +3%
3 Max HP: +15%, Damage increase per Morph Gauge Stage: +4%


Active Dragon Link
Master Level 1
Description Connects Dragon Slash with other special attack skills to grant bonus effects.
Level 1 Morph Gauge fills faster, and the Dragon Link skill and the Kaiser attack skill that follows will have their final damage increased by 15%. Once used, any buff that increases the final damage of following attack will disappear regardless of the skill. Does not apply to Wing Beat.


Active Exclusive Spell
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increases the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby characters.
Cooldown: 300 sec
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: +4%, Duration: 40 min


Active Guardian's Return
Master Level 1
Description Returns you to Pantheon as the Nova Guardian.
Level 1 MP Cost: 100
Cooldown: 600 sec

Kaiser (I)

Show/hide all levels
Active Dragon Slash
Master Level 20
Description Mash the attack key to whip enemies in front of you up to 3 times. Can be used with basic attack key while in Final Form.
Level 20 required to learn Dragon Slash I.
Level 1 1-hit: Attack up to 8 enemies for 51% damage 3 times
2-hit: Up to 6 enemies attack for 31% damage 5 times
3-hit: Up to 6 enemies attack for 41% damage 5 times
Final Form: Up to 8 enemies attack for 141% damage 5 times, Up to 10 enemies attack 6 times after 4th job
20 1-hit: Attack up to 8 enemies for 70% damage 3 times
2-hit: Up to 6 enemies attack for 50% damage 5 times
3-hit: Up to 6 enemies attack for 60% damage 5 times
Final Form: Up to 8 enemies attack for 160% damage 5 times, Up to 10 enemies attack 6 times after 4th job

Active Tempest Blades
Master Level 20
Description Periodically summon 3 swords to track and attack enemies. Moves the swords summoned by Tempest Blades: Charge to target and hit the surrounding enemies. The swords target the enemy with the highest max HP.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 20 required to learn Advanced Tempest Blades.
Level 1 MP Cost: 21, Swords Summoned: 3 per 3 sec
Use Tempest Blades: Charge after summoning to send the swords at the enemy and deal 224% damage with 3 attacks.
Final Form: Number of Attacks: +1
20 MP Cost: 30, Swords Summoned: 3 per 3 sec
Use Tempest Blades: Charge after summoning to send the swords at the enemy and deal 300% damage with 3 attacks.
Final Form: Number of Attacks: +1

Active Wing Beat
Master Level 20
Description Creates a whirlwind that attacks enemies until certain targets are defeated. Dissipates after a short distance or time. Unaffected by attack reflection. Up to two can exist.

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF

Erdas Shower

Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +1]
25 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 55 sec, restores 30% HP when used, able to use 17 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 65 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +5]
30 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 60 sec, restores 35% HP when used, able to use 20 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 60 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +6]

Active True Arachnid Reflection
Master Level 25
Description The collapsing space between the Mirror World and reality become linked with Will's Erda, causing the spider within the mirror to temporarily materialize in reality.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP
Spatial Collapse - Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 15, Once complete, summons True Arachnid Reflection.
True Arachnid Reflection - Duration: 50 sec, Goes into attack mode at set intervals. During attack mode, uses spider legs 10 times to deal 182% damage 8 times. If the spider legs attack one target 5 consecutive times, attack mode will end immediately. 3 sec cooldown after attack mode ends.
Cooldown: 250 sec

Active Bladefall
Master Level 25
Description Your Tempest Blades rain down upon the enemy, oozing deadly magma where they land. When all your Tempest Blades land, you can use the skill once more to bring forth the magma. If the magma hits enemies, it immediately resets Draco Surge's cooldown, and does not apply the cooldown for a certain number of times. This enhancement lasts during the cooldown of Bladefall. Only usable with Tempest Blades summoned. Unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, Each blade strikes for 520% damage 4 times and creates a pool of magma where it lands after 2 sec.
The magma hits up to 12 enemies, dealing 728% damage 6 times, and increases up to 1040% in proportion to the time the blade remained in the ground after landing.
Ignores Draco Surge's cooldown 3 time(s).
Cooldown: 30 sec.
Final Form: Tempest Blades and magma's attack counts increase by 1.
25 MP Cost: 1000, Each blade strikes for 1000% damage 4 times and creates a pool of magma where it lands after 2 sec.
The magma hits up to 12 enemies, dealing 1400% damage 6 times, and increases up to 2000% in proportion to the time the blade remained in the ground after landing.
Ignores Draco Surge's cooldown 3 time(s).
Cooldown: 30 sec.
Final Form: Tempest Blades and magma's attack counts increase by 1.
30 MP Cost: 1000, Each blade strikes for 1100% damage 4 times and creates a pool of magma where it lands after 2 sec.
The magma hits up to 12 enemies, dealing 1540% damage 6 times, and increases up to 2200% in proportion to the time the blade remained in the ground after landing.
Ignores Draco Surge's cooldown 3 time(s).
Cooldown: 30 sec.
Final Form: Tempest Blades and magma's attack counts increase by 1.

Active Draco Surge
Master Level 25
Description Enhance Gigas Wave with the strength of an ancient dragon. The Dragon Warrant launches forward to deal additional attacks to the enemy. Requires recharging time after skill is used.
All enemies, including bosses, will be Slowed when hit by Draco Surge. The Dragon Warrant is unaffected by attack reflection.
Dragon Link: During Attack + Gigas Wave
Required Skill: Gigas Wave Lv. 30+

Active Dragonflare
Master Level 25
Description Call forth an ancient dragon god, and with it flame incarnate. Envelop yourself in flames to burn nearby enemies, and leave Fire Energy in your wake.
If your attack skill successfully hits, the trail of Fire Energy you leave behind will explode to deal AoE damage. Using the skill again while its effect is active will cancel that effect.

If your attack skill successfully hits when the active effect of Dragonflare isn't active, a flame orb will form to deal additional attacks. All Dragonflare attacks are unaffected by attack reflection.
Right-click to toggle the Flame Orb Creation on/off.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, Deals automatic attacks to up to 8 surrounding enemies for 390% damage 6 times periodically for 20 sec.
Fire Energy: Maintained for 5 sec. Upon detonation, the Fire Energy and surroundings near Kaiser will attack up to 10 enemies for 468% damage 6 time(s). Explosion Cooldown: 3.6 sec
Fire Orb: 6 Forms Fire Orb(s) that attack for 364% damage 3 time(s). Re-creation Cooldown: 10 sec
Cooldown: 120 sec
25 MP Cost: 1000, Deals automatic attacks to up to 8 surrounding enemies for 750% damage 6 times periodically for 20 sec.
Fire Energy: Maintained for 5 sec. Upon detonation, the Fire Energy and surroundings near Kaiser will attack up to 10 enemies for 900% damage 6 time(s). Explosion Cooldown: 3.6 sec
Fire Orb: 6 Forms Fire Orb(s) that attack for 700% damage 3 time(s). Re-creation Cooldown: 10 sec
Cooldown: 120 sec
30 MP Cost: 1000, Deals automatic attacks to up to 8 surrounding enemies for 825% damage 6 times periodically for 20 sec.
Fire Energy: Maintained for 5 sec. Upon detonation, the Fire Energy and surroundings near Kaiser will attack up to 10 enemies for 990% damage 6 time(s). Explosion Cooldown: 3.6 sec
Fire Orb: 6 Forms Fire Orb(s) that attack for 770% damage 3 time(s). Re-creation Cooldown: 10 sec
Cooldown: 120 sec

Active HEXA Tempest Blades
Master Level 30
Description Periodically summon 5 swords to track and attack enemies. The swords prioritize the enemy with the highest Max HP first.
The ancient dragon's fury marks enemies hit by these swords. If the dormant dragon mark is hit by HEXA Tempest Blades again, it will awaken, activating Dragon Blow If the enemy is hit with Gigas Wave or Draco Surge.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Required Skill: Advanced Tempest Blades Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 70, Swords Summoned: 5 per 3 sec
Use Tempest Blades: Charge after summoning to send the swords at the enemy and deal 543% damage with 4 attacks, Final Form: Number of Attacks: +1
[Dragon Blow] - Additional Attacks: Damage: 2640%, Number of Attacks: 10
30 MP Cost: 77, Swords Summoned: 5 per 3 sec
Use Tempest Blades: Charge after summoning to send the swords at the enemy and deal 775% damage with 4 attacks, Final Form: Number of Attacks: +1
[Dragon Blow] - Additional Attacks: Damage: 3800%, Number of Attacks: 10

[Dragon Blow] - Additional Attacks: Damage: 3680%, Number of Attacks: 10

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
